restrictions that forbid anyone \mbox{\hyperlink{glew-1_811_80_2_readme_8txt_a2dc22b049b18b41fc6752c847e901e46}{to}} deny \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a991d19148ad6e9de17db79cfe1772956}{you}} these \mbox{\hyperlink{_l_i_c_e_n_s_e_8txt_ad354d4ca04a11d835890c1762f260975}{so}} \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a9e51ef783d8185aecf4c5f1580b91c00}{they}} know their \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a6b5cc11d5b264dc299d9a0af4b4578be}{rights}} We protect your \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a6b5cc11d5b264dc299d9a0af4b4578be}{rights}} with two \mbox{\hyperlink{_l_i_c_e_n_s_e_8txt_a666ac2f420de15eb9624302d6c816d81}{distribute}} \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a11c72046f83d32eec45ef96ef51cc2b7}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a872dd4a12f8937d7c492546c566879a6}{or}} \mbox{\hyperlink{_l_i_c_e_n_s_e_8txt_a329148d81762707519922a898bfbc8db}{modify}} the \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_ab6cadc210adc07b9b9983fb04f314938}{software}} for each author s protection \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a11c72046f83d32eec45ef96ef51cc2b7}{and}} we want \mbox{\hyperlink{glew-1_811_80_2_readme_8txt_a2dc22b049b18b41fc6752c847e901e46}{to}} make certain that everyone understands that there is no \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_af296799e8d4b139b0e400e5ade567f3b}{warranty}} for \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a53f87052a7b055cdeb12d7b8442f26d9}{this}} free \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_ab6cadc210adc07b9b9983fb04f314938}{software}} is modified by someone else \mbox{\hyperlink{gpl_8txt_a11c72046f83d32eec45ef96ef51cc2b7}{and}} passed we want its recipients
